SELECT [e].[EndTime], [e].[LessonId], [t0].[Id] AS [LessonPracticeId], [e].[Name]
FROM [Contests] AS [e]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [e0].*
    FROM [Lessons] AS [e0]
    WHERE [e0].[IsDeleted] = 0
) AS [t] ON [e].[LessonId] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [e1].*
    FROM [Practices] AS [e1]
    WHERE [e1].[IsDeleted] = 0
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[LessonId]
WHERE (([e].[IsDeleted] = 0) AND ([e].[IsDeleted] = 0)) AND ([e].[EndTime] < GETDATE())

FROM [Contests] AS [e]

    FROM [Lessons] AS [e0]
    WHERE [e0].[IsDeleted] = 0
) AS [t] ON [e].[LessonId] = [t].[Id]

    SELECT [e1].*
    FROM [Practices] AS [e1]
    WHERE [e1].[IsDeleted] = 0
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[LessonId]
